<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:басить.html>баси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">basítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробег.html>пробе́г</a> (21993)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробег.html>пробе́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probég</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробег.html>пробе́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробежать.html>пробе́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробег.html>пробе́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>run <i>(distance)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробег.html>пробе́г</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посадка.html>поса́дке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probég</b> pri posádke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">landing run</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> run, race
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лыжный.html>лы́жный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробег.html>пробе́г</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lýžnyj <b>probég</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ski run; ski race</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>total distance passed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробег.html>пробе́г</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probég</b> avtomobílja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mileage; number of kilometres travelled</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробег.html>пробе́г</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́шего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ля</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kakój <b>probég</b> u váševo avtomobílja?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">what mileage has your car done?; how many kilometres has your car travelled/done?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пробегавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробегать.html>пробегавший</a> (7444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробегать.html>пробега́ть</a> (7444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробегать.html>пробега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробежать.html>пробежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run past, to run through</li>
<li>to run a certain distance or for some time</li>
<li>to skim, to scan, to look through</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробегать.html>пробе́гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probégatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spend some time running</li></ol>

***пробежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробежать.html>пробежа́ть</a> (4186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробежать.html>пробежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробегать.html>пробега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run past, to run through</li>
<li>to run a certain distance or for some time</li>
<li>to skim, to scan, to look through</li></ol>

***пробел.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробел.html>пробе́л</a> (15473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бел</a>(ый)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bel(yj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробел.html>пробе́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probél</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробел.html>пробе́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробел.html>пробе́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробел.html>пробе́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>space, blank, gap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нажать.html>нажа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:клавиша.html>кла́вишу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробел.html>пробе́ла</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nažátʹ klávišu <b>probéla</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to press the <b>space</b> key</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>flaw, defect</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a> (11409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to punch out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дыра.html>дыру́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probivátʹ</b> dyrú</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to make/punch/pierce a hole</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probivátʹ</b> bilét</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to punch/cancel a ticket</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pierce, to go <i>(through)</i></li>
<li>to break <i>(through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probivátʹ</b> stenu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">break through a wall</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to make <i>(a road, a tunnel)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туннель.html>тунне́ль</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probivátʹ</b> tunnɛ́lʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to make a tunnel</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probivátʹ</b> dorógu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to break a way</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to issue a check/chit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pay to the cashier</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press <i>(for)</i>, to push <i>(for)</i>, to struggle <i>(for)</i>, to win, to bring off, to put across

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробиваться.html>пробива́ться</a> (5846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиваться.html>пробива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиться.html>проби́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fight/force/make one's way through, to break/win/strike through
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>лучи́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиваться.html>пробива́ются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозь.html>сквозь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́н</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lučí <b>probivájutsja</b> skvozʹ tumán</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">rays struggle through the fog</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиваться.html>пробива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозь.html>сквозь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толпа.html>толпу́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probivátʹsja</b> skvozʹ tolpú</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to make/force/fight/elbow one's way through a crowd</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>трудо́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиваться.html>пробива́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s trudóm <b>probivátʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to struggle through</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shoot, to show, to push up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of plants</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>трава́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начинать.html>начина́ет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиваться.html>пробива́ться</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">travá načinájet <b>probivátʹsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the grass begins to shoot</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***пробирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробирать.html>пробира́ть</a> (23231)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-birátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробирать.html>пробира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пробра́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel strong coldness of the air or wind</li>
<li>to scold</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробираться.html>пробира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробраться.html>пробра́ться</a></b>)

***пробить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a> (3912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*probiti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pro-</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*biti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробивать.html>пробива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to punch out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дыра.html>дыру́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> dyrú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make/punch/pierce a hole</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> bilét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to punch/cancel a ticket</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pierce, to go <i>(through)</i></li>
<li>to break <i>(through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> stenu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">break through a wall</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to make <i>(a road, a tunnel)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туннель.html>тунне́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> tunnɛ́lʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a tunnel</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break a way</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to issue a check/chit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pay to the cashier</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press <i>(for)</i>, to push <i>(for)</i>, to struggle <i>(for)</i>, to win, to bring off, to put across
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрешение.html>разреше́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> razrešénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to struggle to obtain permission</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снижение.html>сниже́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:налог.html>нало́гов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> snižénije nalógov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to push for taxes to be reduced</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:льгота.html>льго́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>probítʹ</b> sebé lʹgótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to win a (hard-to-get) benefit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правительство.html>прави́тельство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спешно.html>спе́шно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поправка.html>попра́вки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́ну</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pravítelʹstvo spéšno <b>probílo</b> poprávki k zakónu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the cabinet rammed/railroaded the amendments to the law</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проба.html>пробой</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">proboj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пробойник</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">probojnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to strike, to sound

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробиться.html>проби́ться</a> (5806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробить.html>проби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиться.html>проби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробиваться.html>пробива́ться</a></b>)

<li><i>(of plants)</i> to shoot, to show, to push up</li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">problema</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πρόβλημα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próblēma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">anything thrown forward, hindrance, obstacle, anything projecting, a headland, promontory</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***проблематичный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проблематичный.html>проблемати́чный</a> (21779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проблематичный.html>проблемати́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">problematíčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>problematic</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проблема.html>пробле́ма</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">probléma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проблемность</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">problemnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проблематичность</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">problematičnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проблематика.html>проблема́тика</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">problemátika</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***пробный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бный</a> (14707)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проба.html>про́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">próbnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sample, trial, test
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:урок.html>урок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>próbnyj</b> urok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">test lesson</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бный</a></b> полёт</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>próbnyj</b> poljót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">test flight</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:раствор.html>раство́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>próbnyj</b> rastvór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">experimental solution</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экземпляр.html>экземпля́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>próbnyj</b> ekzɛmpljár/ekzempljár</i> ― <span class="e-translation">specimen copy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:закупка.html>заку́пка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>próbnaja</b> zakúpka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">trial purchase</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:партия.html>па́ртия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>próbnaja</b> pártija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">trial lot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мень</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>próbnyj</b> kámenʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">touchstone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробный.html>про́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шар.html>шар</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>próbnyj</b> šar</i> ― <span class="e-translation">trial balloon</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***пробовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробовать.html>про́бовать</a> (2611)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проба.html>про́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">próba</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Probe</i>, from Middle Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">proba</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">probō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pro-bhwo-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">being in front</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from *pro-, a variant of the base *per-, + the base *bhu- (to be).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробовать.html>про́бовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">próbovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попробовать.html>попро́бовать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to test, to attempt, to try</li>
<li>to taste (to sample the flavor of something), to feel</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опробовать.html>опро́бовать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opróbovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепробовать.html>перепро́бовать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perepróbovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проба.html>пробой</a> (29528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проба.html>пробо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробой.html>пробо́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробой.html>пробо́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробой.html>пробо́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(for a lock)</i> holdfast, clamp, hasp</li>
<li>rupture, breakdown, punch-through, runaway, puncture, disruption, burst
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проба.html>пробой</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кабель.html>ка́беля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proboj</b> kábelja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cable fault</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проболтаться.html>проболта́ться</a> (19610)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">проболта́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proboltátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проболтаться.html>проболта́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proboltátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проба́лтываться</b>)
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blab, to spill the beans</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">проболта́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proboltátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробор.html>пробо́ров</a></b>)

<ol><li>parting <i>(of hair)</i>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробормотавший.html>пробормота́вший</a> (2238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробормотавший.html>пробормота́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probormotávšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробормотать.html>пробормота́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probormotátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бормотать.html>бормота́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bormotátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробормотать.html>пробормота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probormotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бормотать.html>бормота́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mutter, to murmur, to babble</li></ol>
